PART VI : VeTeRInARy SuRGeonS
LIST of  VeTeRInARy  SuRGeonS  AnD  PRAcTITIoneRS

i, the registrar of the Veterinary Council of sri Lanka notify by the Gazette publication the following Names of Veterinary surgeons registered up to 20.07.2020. at 
the Veterinary Council of sri Lanka, under section 27 (1) of the above act.
